@d1of the width of the Beis Hamikdosh.@d2
@c4@dl@dlרֹחַב הַבָּיִת.@d2
@c3The length of the entrance hall
@c4אֹרֶךְ הָאוּלָם
@c3was along the width of the Sanctuary,
@c4לְרָחְבּוֹ שֶׁל הַהֵיכָל
@c3from north to south.
@c4מִן הַצָּפוֹן לַדָּרוֹם.
@c3All larger measurements
@c4כָּל מִדָּה הַיְתֵרָה
@c3are referred to as the length,
@c4קְרוּיָה אֹרֶךְ,
@c3and the lesser are referred to as the width.
@c4וְהַפְּחוּתָה קְרוּיָה רֹחַב,
@c3Since in the Sanctuary,
@c4לְפִי שֶׁבַּהֵיכָל
@c3the measurement from east to west
@c4מִדַּת מִן הַמִּזְרָח לַמַּעֲרָב
@c3was greater,@nt4
@c4יְתֵרָה,
@c3it was called the length,
@c4קְרוּיָה אֹרֶךְ,
@c3but since the entrance hall’s measurement
@c4וּבָאוּלָם שֶׁמִּדַּת
@c3from north to south was greater,@nt5
@c4מִצָּפוֹן לַדָּרוֹם יְתֵרָה בּוֹ,
@c3[that which is] called the length,
@c4קְרוּיָה אֹרֶךְ
@c3[is the measurement] from north to south
@c4מִן הַצָּפוֹן לַדָּרוֹם,
@c3and [the measurement] from east to west
@c4וּמִן הַמִּזְרָח לַמַּעֲרָב
@c3was called the width.
@c4קְרוּיָה בּוֹ רֹחַב.

@c3[The equivalent of] six thousand @itse’ah@ic,
@c4שֵׁשֶׁת אֲלָפִים סְאִים,
@c3for a @hhבת@ee is equal to three @itse’ah@ic,
@c4שֶׁהַבַּת שָׁלשׁ סְאִין,
@c3as it is stated,
@c4שֶׁנֶּאֱמַר:
@c3“The @hhאיפה@ee and the @hhבת@ee [should] have one measurement.”@nt43
@c4הָאֵיפָה וְהַבַּת תֹכֶן אֶחָד לָהֶם.
@c3Thus, [six thousand @itse’ah@ic] are found to be
@c4נִמְצְאוּ
@c3one hundred fifty ritual baths of purity;
@c4חֲמִשִּׁים וּמֵאָה מִקְוֵה טָהֳרָה,
@c3four thousand @itse’ah@ic for one hundred ritual baths,
@c4הָאַרְבָּעִים מֵאוֹת, מֵאָה מִקְוָאוֹת,
@c3and the two thousand [@itse’ah@ic] for fifty ritual baths.@nt44
@c4וְהָעֶשְׂרִים מֵאוֹת, חֲמִשִּׁים מִקְוָאוֹת.
@c3And even were you to divide everything
@c4וְאַף כְּשֶׁתְּחַלֵּק הַכֹּל
@c3according to the measurement
@c4לְפִי מִדָּה
@c3by which the Sages measured,
@c4שֶׁשִּׁעֲרוּ חֲכָמִים
@c3an @itamoh@ic squared by three @itamohs@ic high
@c4אַמָּה עַל אַמָּה בְּרוּם שָׁלשׁ אַמּוֹת
@c3for each ritual bath,
@c4לַמִּקְוֶה,
@c3you will find it to be the same [as follows]:
@c4תִּמְצֶאנָה כֵּן,
@c3[The lower part of the sea was] three @itamohs@ic high
@c4שָׁלשׁ אַמּוֹת מְרֻבָּעוֹת,
@c3[by one hundred square @itamohs@ic]
@c3equaling one hundred ritual baths.
@c4מֵאָה מִקְוָאוֹת,
@c3The [upper part of the sea was] two
@c4וּשְׁתַּיִם
@c3[@itamohs@ic high and] round [with a diameter of ten @itamohs@ic
@c4@c3הָעֲגֻלּוֹת,
@c3and contained sufficient water for] fifty ritual baths,
@c4חֲמִשִּׁים מִקְוָאוֹת,
@c3because the square is greater than the circle
@c4שֶׁהַמְּרֻבָּע יָתֵר עַל הָעִגּוּל
@c3by one quarter.
@c4רְבִיעִית.
@c3[And in Divrei Hayomim] it is written,
@c4וּבְדִבְרֵי הַיָּמִים כְּתִיב:
@c3“it capacity was three thousand @itbas@ic.”@nt45
@c4בַּתִּים שְׁלשֶׁת אֲלָפִים יָכִיל,
@c3Our Rabbis explained it refers to a dry measure,

@c4וּתְחִלַּת נְפִילָה נִיסָה.
@1P@c4[38@p2]And the dogs licked his blood.
@P1[לח@P2]וַיָּלֹקּוּ הַכְּלָבִים אֶת דָּמוֹ.@d2
@c3I say that
@c4וְאוֹמֵר אֲנִי,
@c3Novos was killed there,

@c3the blood of Navos, etc.”@nt18@nt19
@c4אֶת דַּם נָבוֹת וְגוֹ'.
@d1And they washed the weapons [there].
@c4@D1@D1וְהַזֹּנוֹת רָחָצוּ.@d2

@c3[Targum] Yonoson rendered it in this manner.
@c4כָּךְ תִּרְגֵּם יוֹנָתָן.
@c3But our Rabbis said, “Achov was a cold person,

@c3so Ezevel made for him

@c4דְּמוּת שְׁתֵּי זוֹנוֹת בְּמֶרְכַּבְתּוֹ.
@1P@1P[39@p2]The ivory palace.
@P1[לט@P2]וּבֵית הַשֵּׁן.@d2
@c3[Made of] elephant tooth [i.e., ivory].
@c4שֵׁן דְּפִיל.
@1P[45@p2]Yehoshofot made peace
@P1[מה@P2]וַיַּשְׁלֵם יְהוֹשָׁפָט

@1P[48@p2]There was no king in Edom.
@P1[מח@P2]וּמֶלֶךְ אֵין בֶּאֱדוֹם.@d2

@c4עֲדַיִן הָיוּ כְּפוּפִין לוֹ.
@1P[49@p2]For they [the ships] were broken.

@1P@1P[52@p2]In the seventeenth year of Yehoshofot.

@c3Some wonder about this verse,
@c4יֵשׁ מַתְמִיהִים עַל הַמִּקְרָא הַזֶּה,

@c3@c4However, I searched and found in Divrei Hayomim
@c4אַךְ בָּדַקְתִּי וּמָצָאתִי בְּדִבְרֵי הַיָּמִים
@c3concerning the kings of Yisroel,
@c4לְמַלְכֵי יִשְׂרָאֵל

@c3and if one became king at the end of a year,
@c4וְאִם עָמַד בְּסוֹף שָׁנָה,
@c3he counts it at the beginning,
@c4מוֹנֶה אוֹתָהּ לוֹ בִּתְחִלָּתוֹ,

@c3@c3Therefore I say
@c4לְכָךְ אֲנִי אוֹמֵר,

@c4שֶׁאָמַר
@c3in reference to when Yehoshofot became king,

@c3does not count with it
@c4לֹא נִמְנֵית עִמּוֹ
@c3Achov’s first year [of kingship].
